 ) Congress general secretary Ashok Gehlot lashed out at the central government today
 unhone kaha ki janata ke saath har saal vishwasghaat hua he
 Every year the government spends crores and celebrates and loots public money
 petrol-deazal kii qeemat par hamaare jamaane main tamaasha banaati thi aaj khud janata kii jeb par daaka daal rahi he
 Congress spokesperson Randeep Surjewala Congress said that Congress will celebrate 'betrayal Day' on 26 May to mark the completion of four years of the Narendra Modi government and will 'expose' this government to the public
 surajevaala ne kaha, 'congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi ne varisht netaaon ke saath vichaar-vimarsh karke faisla kiya he ki 26 may diwas ko party vishwasghaat diwas manaayegi
 The betrayal of the Modi government will be exposed to the public
 ' He said that on 26 May, sit-ins and demonstrations will be organized at all state capitals and district levels
 surajevaala ne aarope lagaaya ki yah sarkaar bhrashtachar, kaledhan, mahangaai, aatankwaad or videsh niti ko lekar puri tarah vifal rahi he
 Congress General Secretary Ashok Gehlot released a poster titled 'betrayal'
 gahalot ne kaha, 'media or aam log samaj gaye hai ki unke saath vishwasghaat hua
 Four years ago a lot of promises were made and the public also reposed great faith
 lekin chaar saal main is kadar vishwasghaat hua ki uski kalpana nahin kii ja sakati
 " gahalot ne kaha, ' ye log chaal, charitra or cheharaa alag hone kaa daawa karte the lekin inhone apane hi siddhanton kii dhajjiyaan uda deen

" har varg pareshaan he
 The farmer is upset
 yuva pareshaan he

 sabake saath vishwasghaat hua he

 aaj dekhie ki petrol or dijal kii keemat kahaan pahunch gai

 ' Gehlot said that Rahul Gandhi demanded that the price of petrol and diesel be brought under the purview of GST, but this government was not ready
 unhone aarope lagaaya, 'ye paakhandee, fasivadi log hai

 daliton par atyaachaar bad gaye hai
 Cases of sexual violence on women and girls are increasing

 The question is, how do you form a government? This means that these people would buy and sell
 tippaniyan Gehlot alleged, 'piyush Goyal sold his 10 rupees shares for 10 thousand rupees and Vasundhara Raje's son sold 10 rupees shares to Lalit Modi for about one lakh rupees
 in maamalon kii jaanch kyon nahin hui

 guwahati main purvottar parishad ke 68veen purna satr ko bataur chairman sambodhit karte hue ravivaar(8 sitambar) ko grih mantri amit shah ne purvottar ke aath rajyon ke mukhyamantriyon se kaha ki anuchhed 371 samvidhan kii vishesh vyavastha he or bijepi sarkaar iskaa sammaan karti he or isamen kisi tarah kaa badlaav nahin kiya jayega
 Earlier on August 6, Amit Shah had given a similar assurance in the Lok Sabha
 amit shah ne baithak main yah bhi kaha ki aazaadee ke baad baaki desh ke 70 saal ke vikaas kii tulana main uttar-purv kaa 5 saal kaa vikaas kahin adhik he or aaj narendra modi sarkaar main uttar-purv vikaas ke liye janaa jaataa he
 In many arguments in favor of 371 when Amit Shah also raised the issue of Article 371 on August 6 during the debate on 370, during the debate, Home Minister Amit Shah made many arguments as to why the government does not want to remove this article

 of Nagas
 yah anuchhed desh kii ekta or akhandta kii raah main baadhak nahin he

 Amit Shah also said in Lok Sabha on August 6, "the core of Section 371 is to create boards for Maharashtra, Gujarat, Vidarbha, Marathwada, Saurashtra and Kutch
" aise main 371 se kisi ko kya aapatti he
 Why would we remove him? ?kya he anuchhed 371purvottar sahit desh ke kareeb 11 rajyon main anuchhed 371 ke vibhinn praavdhaan lagu he
 With the help of this article, the central government can work related to development, security, safety etc
 in the respective states
 yani ek prakaar se yah anuchhed sambandhit rajyon ko vishesh darja jaisi vyavastha detaa he

 in ilaakon main vikaas kaary ke liye baraabar fund diya jayega

 isamen raashtrapati ke paas yah adhikaar hota he ki vah rajya sarkaar ko aadesh de ki kis job main kis varg ke logon ko naukari di ja sakati he

 ye cameti rajya ke vikaas sambandhi kaaryon kii nigaraanee karegi

 mizo samudaay kii paramparaon, shaskeey, naagarik or aapraadhik nyaay sambandhi niyamon ko bharat sarkaar kii sansad nahin badal sakati

 nagaland main 371e lagu he
